Additionally,  completing some tasks will grant you a limited number of Pact resets</col>,  which will allow you to reset your talent tree.|Each area has an Echo Boss,  these are enhanced bosses that pose a higher challenge and drop new unique rewards. Killing the regular boss may drop an Echo orb that lets you access the Echo variant. More information can be found in the area interfaces.|Leagues VI:  Demonic pacts will run from April 15th until the game update on <span style="color: #6bc71f">11th</span> June.', '1': 'Your character is an Ironman,  meaning you cannot trade with other players.|You will start off with Varlamore unlocked.|You will auto complete the following quests: <br>- Desert Treasure 2 (no Pre-reqs)<br>- Dragon Slayer<br>- Rune Mysteries<br>- Druidic Ritual<br>- Fairytale Part II (all pre-reqs)<br>- Elemental Workshop I<br>- Lost City<br>- Nature Spirit<br>- Elemental Workshop I<br>- Perilous Moons<br>- Priest in Peril<br>- Twilight's Promise|You will start with the following stat increases: |- 3 Herblore<br>- 5 Runecraft|A Dramen Staff will be added to your Inventory so that you can access Fairy rings. If lost,  you can reclaim it from the Leagues tutor in Yama's lair.', '2': 'Echo Boss Rewards are a guaranteed drop if you exceed 2x the drop rate.|Slayer Masters will assign you tasks taking into account the areas you have currently unlocked.|Teleports and transportation methods to locations outside of areas you have unlocked are restricted.|When purchasing your Player Owned House it will be accessible from Aldarin. Your house can only be moved to areas you have unlocked.|Unlocking new areas will complete various quests and Achievement Diary tasks but will not award any quest completion XP. However,  you may complete some quests on your own to gain their XP before unlocking the area which auto-completes it.|Most shop stock will not deplete.|The following shop stocks have been modified: <br>- Elemental Shields have been added to all Slayer Equipment shops<br>- Box traps and Bird snares will be available to buy in the Civitas general stores|Impling spawn rates have been increased.|Rarity of rare implings has been increased.|Dragon implings drop reduced Dragon Bones.|All Soulreaper Axe pieces will drop from every Desert Treasure 2 Boss.|Pets and any pet transmog items that roll over between leagues do not count towards the collection log tasks.|The Twisted Bow,  Scythe of Vitur,  and Tumeken's Shadow are available from all three raids.|Items that drop as components that require multiple regions to create a usable item will drop as the finished item.|CoX:  CM,  ToB:  HM and ToA 500+ have significantly buffed drop rates and difficulty,  ToA and ToB will now provide uniques to all players in the raid if the raid obtains one.|Pet Transmogs will now roll over between leagues.|The Leagues tutor in Yama's lair can sell Max Capes once you are eligible.|Nihil Shards drop in increased quantity from Nex.|Scythe of Vitur can be charged with just blood runes.|Zulrah has no damage cap or melee damage immunity.|Forestry Events are three times as likely to spawn.|Wilderness Bosses can be accessed without the Wilderness Medium Diary.|The Abyss and Zanaris are now counted as general regions,  meaning you can access them from anywhere via a fairy ring (This includes the cosmic altar).'}
|}
